PREFACE
         This code of the Village of Dieterich, as supplemented, contains
ordinances up to and including ordinance 1191-2025, passed April 7, 2025.
Ordinances of the Village adopted after said ordinance supersede the provisions
of this code to the extent that they are in conflict or inconsistent therewith.
Consult the Village office in order to ascertain whether any particular
provision of the code has been amended, superseded or repealed.
                     American Legal Publishing
                     Cincinnati, Ohio
ORDINANCES PENDING REVIEW FOR CODIFICATION
Listed ordinances have been passed, but they are pending review by the
publisher, and they may not affect the code of ordinances. Additionally,
ordinances listed in this section may not show the original ordinances in their
entirety. Please contact the office of the clerk if there are any questions
concerning any listed ordinances.
ORDINANCE NO. __1196-2025______
AN ORDINANCE REGULATING THE VILLAGE OF DIETERICH CEMETERY IN THE VILLAGE OF
DIETERICH, ILLIINOIS
 
WHEREAS, the Village of Dieterich, Illinois, is authorized, pursuant to 65 ILCS
5/11-49-1, to establish and regulate cemeteries within or without the municipal
limits of the Village of Dieterich, Illinois; and,
 
   WHEREAS, the Board of Trustees of the Village of Dieterich, Illinois, after
careful investigation and consideration, has determined that it is in the best
interest of the Village of Dieterich, Illinois, to establish regulations for
the orderly and efficient administration of the Village of Dieterich Cemetery
within the corporate limits of the Village of Dieterich, Illinois.
 
   NOW, THEREFORE, BE IT HEREBY ORDAINED BY THE BOARD OF TRUSTEES OF THE
VILLAGE OF DIETERICH, ILLINOIS, THAT:
 
SECTION 1:   The preliminary paragraphs set forth above are incorporated herein
as part of this Ordinance.
 
SECTION 2:    TITLE: This Ordinance shall be known and cited as the “Village of
Dieterich Cemetery Ordinance.”
 
SECTION 3: DEFINITIONS:  The following words, terms and phrases, when used in
this Ordinance, shall have the meanings ascribed to them in this Section,
except where the context clearly indicates a different meaning:
 
A.   “Cemetery” shall mean, for the purposes of these rules and regulations,
the whole designated area set aside and apart for the burial of human remains
by earth interment, or by interment in a mausoleum, crypt, or urn.
 
B.   “Cremation” shall mean the process whereby a body is reduced to ashes.
 
C.   “Cremains” shall mean the container and incinerated body of a deceased
person.
 
D.   “Crypt” shall mean a vault or chamber which is wholly or partly beneath
the surface of the earth.
 
E.   “Grave” shall mean an excavation in the earth for the burial of remains,
as well as including the burial place in a tomb or sepulcher.
 
F.   “Gravestone” shall mean a stone with an inscription erected near the grave
or laying over it.
 
G.   “Interment” shall mean the act of depositing remains in the earth, tomb,
or burial vault.
 
H.   “Lot” shall mean a part of the Cemetery intended for burial and embraces
more grounds than a single grave.
 
I.   “Mausoleum” shall mean a building in which remains are deposited above the
ground.
 
J.   “Memorial” shall mean anything intended to preserve the memory of a
person, including a monument, which may be a stone or building or something
else which is either erected or maintained to preserve the memory of a person.
 
K.   “Person” shall mean any natural person, firm, partnership, joint venture,
club, company, association, syndicate, society, business trust, organization,
institution, agency, government corporation, municipal corporation, district or
other political subdivision, corporation, limited liability company,
proprietorship, contractor, supplier, vendor, vendee, operator, or other legal
entity. It shall also include an executor, administrator, trustee, receiver or
other representative appointed according to law. Whenever the word "Person"
appears in any section of this Ordinance prescribing a penalty or fine, as to
partnerships or associations, the word shall include the partners or members
thereof, and as to corporations or limited liability company, shall include the
officers, agents or members thereof who are responsible for any violation of
this Ordinance.
 
L.   “Tomb” shall mean a vault or chamber which is partly or entirely above the
ground where remains are interred.
 
M.   “Vault” shall mean a chamber constructed of concrete or steel used to
enclose a casket.
 
N.   “Village” shall mean the Village of Dieterich, Illinois, an Illinois
municipal corporation.
 
SECTION 4:     APPLICABILITY OF THIS ORDINANCE:
 
A.   This Ordinance shall apply only to a Cemetery owned,
controlled, or operated by the Village.
 
B.    The provisions of this Ordinance shall not apply to Village
officials, or their agents or designees involved with the upgrading,
maintenance, administration, or care of a Village Cemetery.
 
C.   The provisions of this Ordinance shall not apply to police
officers or firefighting officials or officers involved in carrying
out their official duties.
 
SECTION 5: SPECIAL EXCEPTION PROVISIONS:
 
A.    Special circumstances may arise in which the literal enforcement of the
regulations, as contained in this Ordinance, may impose unnecessary hardship.
The Village Board of Trustees, therefore, reserves the right to make
exceptions, suspensions, or modifications to any of the regulations contained
in this Ordinance, without notice, and such temporary exception, suspension or
modification shall in no way be construed as affecting the general application
of such regulations.
 
B.    The Village Board of Trustees hereby expressly reserves the right to
adopt additional rules and regulations, and further expressly reserves the
right to amend, alter, or repeal any rule, regulation, section, paragraph, or
part thereof, of this Ordinance, at any time.
 
SECTION 6:    SALE OF CEMETERY LOTS; NONTRANSFERABLE:
 
A.    After the effective date of this Ordinance, Cemetery Lots within a
Cemetery shall be sold by the Village
for the purpose of burial for the purchaser of a Cemetery Lot, or his
or her immediate family. No sale shall be made to funeral directors or others,
except for those acting as an agent for an eligible purchaser. For the purpose
of this Ordinance, the term "immediate family" shall be defined as spouse,
child, stepchild, son-in-law, daughter-in-law, parent, stepparent, parent-in-
law, half or full brothers and sisters, by blood or in law relation.
 
B.    All sales and transfers of a Cemetery Lot shall be made in the form of a
cemetery quitclaim deed and signed by the Village President, or his or her
designee, and attested by the Village Clerk. The cemetery quitclaim deed shall
contain a provision that the conveyance of the Cemetery Lot is made in strict
compliance with the provisions of this Ordinance, as may be amended from time
to time, or any other regulations pertaining to the management, supervision, or
upkeep of Lots within a Cemetery.
 
C.    Cemetery Lots are nontransferable without prior written approval by the
Village. No transfer of any Lot shall be made directly by any Cemetery Lot
owner, his or her heirs, devisees, or successors to any person, unless
registered with the Village Clerk.  A Cemetery Lot may be sold
back for the original purchase price to the Village (for resale by the
Village). The original deed is required to be provided to the Village when the
Cemetery Lot is sold back to the Village.
 
D.   The Village Board of Trustees shall have the authority to place a limit
on the number of Cemetery Lots sold to a particular person, as
well as such person’s family
and relatives. Furthermore, the Village shall have the absolute right and discretion
to determine whether a particular Cemetery Lot or Lots
will be sold to a specific person and where such Cemetery Lot or Lots will
be located within the Cemetery.  Such decision shall be based on factors,
including, but not limited to, the number of vacant Cemetery Lots available and
whether family or relatives of the person seeking to purchase a Cemetery
Lot or Lots are buried adjacent or nearby the Cemetery Lot or Lots requested.
 
E.    The lawful owner of any Cemetery Lot within a Cemetery
shall promptly provide the Village Clerk with any change in that owner’s
mailing address.
 
SECTION 7: CORRECTION OF ERRORS: The Village reserves, and
shall have, the right to correct any errors that may be made by the Village
concerning interments, disinterments, or removals, or in the description,
transfer, or conveyance of any Cemetery Lot, either by requiring that a
particular vacant Cemetery Lot or Lots be conveyed back to the Village and
conveying in lieu thereof another vacant Cemetery Lot or Lots in a similar
location within the Cemetery
at issue or by refunding the money paid for the Cemetery Lot or Lots
 to the purchaser or the successor of the purchaser.  In the event that an
error involves the interment of the remains of any person, the Village
shall have the right to remove and transfer the remains so interred to
another Cemetery Lot in a similar location in the same Cemetery in
accordance with law.
 
SECTION 8: PURCHASE PRICE FOR CEMETERY LOT:
 
A.    The purchase price for each Cemetery Lot shall be established by the
Village Board of Trustees from time to time, with a copy of the purchase price
being available at the office of the Village Clerk. The purchase price shall be
paid to the Village Treasurer.
 
B.    The Village Board of Trustees may periodically increase the purchase
price of a Cemetery Lot to accommodate increased costs and needed reserve funds
for Cemetery maintenance.
 
SECTION 9: MARKERS, MEMORIALS AND MONUMENTS:
 
A.    Quality Materials. To properly perpetuate memory, all Memorials and
Monuments shall be of quality granite, marble, or other natural stone, or other
equally durable composition and be of dignified design. Makeshift
memorials will not be permitted.
 
B.    Location: All Memorials and Monuments, or other markers shall be placed
only at the head of the gravesite. Footstones are prohibited. This regulation
shall not apply to the memorials in place prior to the effective date of this
Ordinance but represents an ideal to be attained. Where continuous runners have
been installed, all Memorials and Monuments shall be placed on top the runner.
 
C.    Foundation: Where continuous runners have been installed, no monument
foundation will be required, and Memorials and Monuments shall be installed on
the runner. Where there are no runners yet installed, the foundation will be
the responsibility of the Cemetery Lot owner(s).
 
D.    Maintenance: The maintenance, repair, and upkeep of a Cemetery memorial,
monument, marker, urn, or similar item is the responsibility of the heirs or
family of the person buried at that Lot. The heirs or family of the person
buried at that Lot shall also be responsible for repairing any settling of any
such memorial, monument, marker, urn or similar item. The Village has no
responsibility or liability regarding the repair, maintenance, or upkeep
regarding any such memorial, monument, marker, urn or similar item.
 
E.    Village Reservation Right: Should any Monument or Memorial, including
any Monument or Memorial that was in place before the effective date of this
Ordinance, become unsightly, broken, moved off its proper site, dilapidated, or a safety
hazard, the Village shall have the right, at the expense
of the owner of the Cemetery Lot, to
correct the condition or remove the same. The Village shall make reasonable
attempts to contact the owner of the Cemetery Lot prior to
any such work beginning.
 
SECTION 10: RECORDS, ADMINISTRATIVE FEES, AND APPROVAL- INTERNMENT AND
DISINTERNMENT:
 
A.    The Village Clerk, and/or his or her designee shall maintain records
concerning all internments, disinternments, Cemetery Lots, and any and all
other records of the Village related to the Village Cemetery.
 
B.    No internment or disinternment shall be permitted on any Lot in the
Village Cemetery until an administrative fee of $200.00 has been paid to the
Village, which said fee being made payable to the Village Treasurer.
 
C.    No
Cemetery Lot shall be opened or closed except under the direction and control of the Village
of Dieterich or such other individual as is designated by the Village
Board. This Paragraph (B) shall not apply to any grave opening,
disinterment, or similar action which is done pursuant to a
valid court order or under the supervision and direction of local
or state health department authorities; however,
even in such cases, the Village of Dieterich shall be given at least twenty-
four (24) hours’ prior notice of when such grave opening or closing will occur.
 
SECTION 11: INTERMENT REGULATIONS:
 
A.    Cemetery Lots are for human remains only.
The following burial combinations are allowed currently per Cemetery Lot
burial (1) one coffin burial, (2) one cremation burial, (3) one coffin and one
cremation burial, or (4) two cremation burials.
 
B.    The Village shall be given no less than a 36-hour notice in advance of
any funeral. The opening and closing of Cemetery Lots shall be done by a
designee of the funeral director upon consultation with the Village.
 
C.    The Village Cemetery will be open for Interments from 8:00 a.m. until 4:
00 p.m. daily.
 
 
 
D.    When an interment is made in a Lot, the location of such interment shall
be designated by the Lot owner. Should the Lot owner fail or neglect to make
such designation, the Village reserves the right to make the Interment at a
location agreed upon by the funeral director and the Village.
 
E.    The Clerk of the Village of Dieterich and/or his or her designee,
must be satisfied, from his or her records, that the deceased person to be
buried in the Cemetery Lot is an authorized
and appropriate person for that space before any interment is
commenced or completed.
 
F.    All interments will require the use of a concrete liner or vault, which
meets all applicable laws. Said concrete liner or vault shall be installed or
constructed in each Cemetery Lot before internment.
 
G.    The interment of Cremains may be made in a Cemetery Lot in a concrete
liner or vault, which meet all applicable laws. No cremains shall be scattered
or dispersed within a Village Cemetery.
 
H.    The surface of all graves shall be kept in an orderly and neat-
appearing manner within the confines of the Cemetery Lot involved.
 
I.    In addition to being subject to the regulations as contained in this
Ordinance, all Interments are made subject to the orders and laws of properly
constituted public officials.
 
SECTION 12: DISINTERMENTS:
 
A.    No disinterment or digging up of an occupied grave shall occur until and
unless any and all permits and licenses and written
authorizations required by law for such disinterment
or digging up of an occupied grave have been obtained from any applicable state
or county agency, governmental unit or official, and a copy
of the same has been filed with the Village.
 
B.    The Village Board of Trustees shall
have the authority to refuse to allow a disinterment or the digging up of an
occupied grave (and to refuse to issue a Village disinterment permit for the
same) if the disinterment or digging up of an occupied grave is
not done pursuant to a court order, issued by a court of
competent jurisdiction, or does not have a reasonable basis.
 
C.    In addition to being subject to the regulations as contained in this
Ordinance, all Disinterment’s and removals are made subject to the orders and
laws of properly constituted public officials.
 
 
 
SECTION 13: GROUNDS MAINTENANCE:
 
A.    No live planting of trees, shrubs, plants, or flowers will be permitted,
except for any trees, shrubs plants, or flowers specifically installed and
maintained by the Village.
 
B.    No decorative rock or landscaping will be permitted in a Village
Cemetery, except for any rocked or landscaping areas installed by the Village.
 
C.   Flowers may be placed on the headstones, or in a shepherd’s hook or other
secured arrangement in close proximity to a Monument or Marker. Except for
markers, memorials, flowers, and urns expressly allowed by this Ordinance,
 and veteran flags as authorized by law, no other item (including,
but not limited to, ornaments, signs, solar lights,
trellises, statues, landscaping, bricks, stones, grave border
materials or other structures) shall be installed or maintained within a
Village Cemetery. Notwithstanding the foregoing, figurines may be placed on a
Monument, but should be glued down or permanently secured in a comparable
method. Notwithstanding anything contained herein to the contrary, where
continuous runners have been installed, all secured arrangements, Memorials and
Monuments, flowers, urns, etc. shall be placed on top the runner.
 
D.    No grading, leveling, digging, mounding, excavating, or similar
alteration of ground or earth is allowed within a Village Cemetery except as
authorized by this Ordinance, or without the prior permission of the Village.
 
E.    All winter artificial wreaths and sprays will be removed by May 1.
 
F.    All summer artificial wreaths and sprays will be removed by October 1.
 
G.    Surfaces other than earth or sod are prohibited.
 
H.    All refuse of any
kind or nature including, but not limited to, dried flowers, wreaths, and
papers and plastic flower containers must be removed from the Village Cemetery,
by the heirs or family of the person buried at the
Lot, within 30 days after a burial.
 
I.    No glass containers or items are allowed.
 
J.   The Village reserves the right to remove
or trim any existing trees, plants or shrubs located within a Village
Cemetery in the interest of maintaining proper appearance and the use of the
Village Cemetery. Furthermore, the Village, and its agents, shall
have the right and authority to remove and dispose
of any and all growth, emblems, displays, containers and other
items that through decay, deterioration, damage or otherwise become or
are unsightly, a source of litter or a maintenance problem.
 
SECTION 14:  PROHIBITED USES AND ACTIVITIES: The following prohibitions
shall apply within any Village Cemetery:
 
A.    No Person shall destroy, deface, apply graffiti to, or otherwise injure
any Monument, Marker, sign, tree, or other lawful item located within a Village
Cemetery.
 
B.    No Person shall disturb the peace
or unreasonably annoy, harass, or disturb any other person who
is lawfully present on the grounds of any Village Cemetery.
 
C.   There shall be no disturbing of the peace or engaging
in any loud or boisterous conduct. Furthermore, there
shall be no unlawful interference with or disruption
of a lawful funeral or funeral procession.
 
D.    No vehicle shall be permitted to drive on any portion of a Village
Cemetery except the designated roads or drives.
 
E.   There shall be no possession or consumption of any alcoholic beverage in a
Village Cemetery.
 
F.    There shall be no music, playing of any radio, or the use
of any amplification device or similar item, except during a burial ceremony or
funeral or a military ceremony.
 
G.    There shall be no littering or dumping in a Village Cemetery.
 
H.   There shall be no fires, candles, or open flames.
 
I.    There shall be no domestic animals of any kind or pets allowed within a
Village Cemetery provided, however, that this prohibition shall not apply to
service dogs or other animals.
 
J.    No firearms or archery arrows shall be discharged or shot except that
military or other veterans’ organizations may carry arms
for the purpose of firing over the grave at the burial of a member.
 
SECTION 15:  CEMETERY HOURS: Unless otherwise specified by the Village Board of
Trustees, a Village Cemetery shall be closed during the hours from 9:
00 p.m. until 7:
00 a.m. the next morning. During those hours, no person shall be present in a Village
Cemetery. Such prohibition on being present in a Village Cemetery
during the time when a Village Cemetery is closed shall not apply to any
Village official, a person accompanied by the Village official, or any law
enforcement or firefighting official when engaged in the lawful duties of
any such office or position.
 
SECTION 16:  DISCLAIMER OF VILLAGE LIABILITY AND RESPONSIBILITY:
Every Person who enters, remains in and travels within a Village
Cemetery does so at their own risk. The Village is not responsible for
any injury, accident or other calamity that might occur to any
person present in a Village Cemetery.  Furthermore, the Village is not
responsible for any damage or vandalism to, theft of or deterioration of any
burial monument, headstone, flower, urn, or other item placed at or near a
Cemetery Lot, burial site or anywhere in a Village Cemetery.  The purchaser
or transferee of any Cemetery Lot or the equivalent (and
all subsequent transferees, assigns, heirs, or beneficiaries)
hereby releases, waives, indemnifies, and holds harmless the Village for, from
and against any injury, damages, causes of action, claims, costs and expenses
associated with, relating to and/or involving the Cemetery Lot
or similar right, any headstone,
monument or similar items, and any matter related to the Cemetery involved.
Such waiver, release and hold harmless provision shall apply not only to the
Village, but also as to all Village employee, officer, official or agent.
 
SECTION 17:  AUTHORITY  OF THE VILLAGE TO REMOVE UNAUTHORIZED OR UNLAWFUL
 ITEMS FROM A VILLAGE CEMETERY: Any monument, marker, planting,
trellis, personal item, urn, flowers or foliage (whether real or artificial),
structure, flag (except for lawful veterans flags), or other item that has
been placed, installed, left or maintained in any Village
Cemetery in violation of this Ordinance, any Village rule or regulation
regarding Village Cemeteries, or any county, state or
federal law, statute or regulation may be removed by the Village from the
Village Cemetery at any time and destroyed or disposed of by the Village
without any prior notice to, permission from, or liability or
obligation to the person or persons who left, installed, maintained or
kept such item in the Village Cemetery. No such item (including, but not
limited to, a monument, marker, planting, solar light,
trellis, personal item, urn, flowers or foliage,
structure, flag, or similar item) can be installed, placed, maintained, or
kept in a Village Cemetery unless expressly authorized by this Ordinance
or a written rule or policy of the Village.  Even if such an item is authorized
to be installed, kept, maintained, or left in a Village Cemetery,
the Village shall still have the discretion to remove any such item at any time
and dispose of the same without prior notice to, consent from or liability
to the Person who installed, maintained or left such item in a Village
Cemetery.
 
SECTION 18: PENALTIES: Any Person which violates, disobeys, omits, neglects, or
refuses to comply with any of the provisions of this Ordinance shall, upon
conviction thereof, be deemed guilty of a civil ordinance violation and shall
be fined not less than Two Hundred Fifty Dollars ($250.00) nor more than Seven
Hundred Fifty Dollars ($750.00) for each offense. A separate offense shall be
deemed to be committed on each day during or on which a violation occurs or
continues. In addition to any fine, the Village may seek injunctive and
declaratory relief directing the violator(s) to cure the violation, and the
Village may revoke any permit authorized and issued pursuant to this Ordinance.
Every act or omission of whatsoever nature constituting a violation of any
provision of this Ordinance, by any officer, director, manager or other agent
or employee of any Person, shall be deemed and held to be the act of such
Person, and the Person shall be punishable in the same manner as if the act or
omission had been done or omitted by him personally.
 
SECTION 19: MISCELLANEOUS PROVISIONS:
 
A.   Invalidity. In the event a court of competent jurisdiction declares any
particular provision of this ordinance to be invalid or unenforceable, the
remaining provisions of this Ordinance shall be construed to be valid and
enforceable. The invalidity of any part of this Ordinance shall not affect any
other part or parts thereof.
 
B.   Effective Date. This Ordinance shall be in full effect from and after
passage and approval as provided by law.
 
C.   Any ordinance of the Village of Dieterich contrary to the terms and
conditions of this Ordinance shall be deemed to be repealed.
